country_event = {
	id = divide_turkey.2 # Iran Wants Us To Embargo Turkey (for russia)
	title = divide_turkey.2.t
	desc = divide_turkey.2.d
	picture = GFX_TUR_generic
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = divide_turkey.2.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:divide_turkey.2.o1 executed"
		SOV = {
			send_embargo = TUR
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = divide_turkey.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = divide_turkey.2.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:divide_turkey.2.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		PER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = small_decrease
			}
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = divide_turkey.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = development_plan.1 # The Third Development Plan
	title = development_plan.1.t
	desc = development_plan.1.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Industry
		name = development_plan.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o1 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = industry_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_industry
	}
	option = { # Science
		name = development_plan.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o2 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = science_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_science
	}
	option = { # Military
		name = development_plan.1.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o3 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = military_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_military
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reorganize_school.1
	title = reorganize_school.t
	desc = reorganize_school.d
	picture = GFX_school_reorganize
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.a
		log = "l"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_3
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.c
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_4
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = PER_contact_k.2 # Iran requests nuke tech: Iran
	title = PER_contact_k.2.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.2.desc
	picture = GFX_KOR_nuke_deal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #offer money
		name = PER_contact_k.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_k.2.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 4
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = PER
						has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
					}
				}
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_contact_k.3
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #offer resources
		name = PER_contact_k.2.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = PER
						has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
					}
				}
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_contact_k.4
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #offer tech
		name = PER_contact_k.2.c
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = PER
						has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
					}
				}
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_contact_k.5
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #no deal
		name = PER_contact_k.2.d
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_k.2.d executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
			}
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_contact_k.7
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = PER_contact_k.6 # Deal goes through
	title = PER_contact_k.6.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.6.d
	picture = GFX_KOR_nuke_deal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #accept tech
		name = PER_contact_k.6.a
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_tech_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					bonus = 0.15
					uses = 2
					category = industry
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_resource_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				create_import = {
					resource = oil
					amount = 16
					exporter = PER
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_moni_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			PER = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_k.6.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		PER = {
			set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_2
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = PER_contact_k.7 # Iran goes to NK
	title = PER_contact_k.7.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.7.d
	picture = GFX_hung_2020
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #contact NK
		name = PER_contact_k.7.a
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
			}
			country_exists = NKO
		}
		NKO = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_contact_nk.1
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #No one else
		name = PER_contact_k.7.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
					has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
					has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = NKO
				}
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_1
		}
	}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_k.7.c
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_2
	}
}

				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_tech_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					add_tech_bonus = {
						bonus = 0.15
						uses = 2
						category = industry
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_resource_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					create_import = {
						resource = oil
						amount = 16
						exporter = PER
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_moni_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 10 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
				PER = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_nk.6.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		PER = {
			set_country_flag = PER_NKO_nd_2
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = PER_contact_with_countries.36.o1 # It's time to change...

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
		add_popularity = { # Increase Emerging
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = communism
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.2
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_opinion_modifier = {
						target = PER
						modifier = no_diplomatic_ties
					}

						remove_opinion_modifier = {
							target = TUR
							modifier = no_diplomatic_ties
						}
						break_embargo = TUR
					}
					SOV = {
						break_embargo = TUR
					}
					ARM = {
						break_embargo = TUR
					}
					TUR = {
						NATO_leave = yes
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } }
							hidden_effect = {
								clear_array = ruling_party
								clear_array = gov_coalition_array
								add_to_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
								update_government_coalition_strength = yes
								update_party_name = yes
								set_coalition_drift = yes
								set_ruling_leader = yes
								set_leader = yes
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = communism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
							set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
							set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
							add_relative_party_popularity = yes
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
							set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
							set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
							set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
							add_relative_party_popularity = yes
						}

						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = USA }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = GER }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ENG }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes
					}
				}
			}
			60 = {
				hidden_effect = {
					NATO_leave = yes
					set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
					set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 1.00 }
					add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } }
						hidden_effect = {
							clear_array = ruling_party

							update_government_coalition_strength = yes
							update_party_name = yes
							set_coalition_drift = yes
							set_ruling_leader = yes
							set_leader = yes

						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = communism
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
						set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
						set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
						add_relative_party_popularity = yes
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
						set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
						set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
						set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
						add_relative_party_popularity = yes
					}

					set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }

		}

			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_half_billion_weekly
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { PER = { has_country_flag = PER_ask_iraq_for_one_billion_weekly } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_one_billion_weekly_money_TT
			PER = { set_country_flag = PER_iraq_accepted_to_pay_one_billion_weekly }
			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_one_billion_weekly
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { PER = { has_country_flag = PER_ask_iraq_for_two_billion_weekly } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_two_billion_weekly_money_TT
			PER = { set_country_flag = PER_iraq_accepted_to_pay_two_billion_weekly }
			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_two_billion_weekly
		}
		hidden_effect = { PER = { country_event = { id = PER_contact_with_countries.54 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_contact_with_countries.52.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_with_countries.52.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_iran_attack_iraq_wargoal_TT
		hidden_effect = { PER = { country_event = { id = PER_contact_with_countries.53 } } }
	}
}

	modify_treasury_effect = yes
		build_railway = {
		  level = 1
		  path = { 9893 3899 11746 11810 9830 9763 9755 940 11860 9878 3983 3951 3786 11811 11829 9833 }
		  start_province = 9893
		  target_province = 9833
		}
		TUR = {
			add_ideas = { PER_TUR_shia_influence }
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 9 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		GRE = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_orupa.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
		BUL = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_orupa.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
	name = PER_orupa.2.b
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_orupa.2.b executed"
	}
}

				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Saudi Arabia is mad
	id = PER_nuclear_compromise.18
	title = PER_nuclear_compromise.18.t
	desc = PER_nuclear_compromise.18.d
	picture = GFX_hung_2020

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #supports american decision
	name = PER_nuclear_compromise.18.a
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_nuclear_compromise.18.a executed"
	}
	option = { #disagree
	name = PER_nuclear_compromise.18.b
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_nuclear_compromise.17.b executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = note_of_protest
		}
	}
	option = { #hostility
	name = PER_nuclear_compromise.18.c
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_nuclear_compromise.18.c executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = loyal_to_our_enemy
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = supports_us
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Iran gets sanctions
	id = PER_sanctions_event.1
	title = PER_sanctions_event.1.t
	desc = PER_sanctions_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_iran_sanctions

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #dam
	name = PER_sanctions_event.1.a
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_sanctions_event.1.a executed"
	unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_resistance_economy
	add_ideas = { PER_economic_sanctions }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PER_resistance_econ
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = GER_mediation_support
						}
					}
				}
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						id = PER_sanctions_event.2
						days = 100
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}
}

# axis_of_resistance_events

country_event = {
	id = axis_of_resistance_events.1 # Iran Wants Us To Join Axis Of Resistance
	title = axis_of_resistance_events.1.t
	desc = axis_of_resistance_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_axis_of_resistance_country

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Together we're stronger!
		name = axis_of_resistance_events.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:axis_of_resistance_events.1.o1 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		PER = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		news_event = {
			id = axis_of_resistance_events.3
			days = 0
		}
		PER = {
			clr_country_flag = invited_syria
			clr_country_flag = invited_iraq
			clr_country_flag = invited_houthis
			clr_country_flag = invited_hezbollah
			clr_country_flag = invited_azerbaijan
			clr_country_flag = invited_turkey
		}
	}
	option = { # No.
		name = axis_of_resistance_events.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:axis_of_resistance_events.1.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = -1
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = axis_of_resistance_events.2
				days = 0
			}
			clr_country_flag = invited_syria
			clr_country_flag = invited_iraq

### Iranian Presidental Elections Events ###

country_event = { # Event to automatically choose presidents based on popularity and date
	id = PER_election_events.1
	title = PER_election_events.1.t
	desc = PER_election_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_election
	trigger = {
		tag = PER
		has_government = communism
		OR = {
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		}
		OR = {
			date > 2001.2.1
			date > 2005.2.1
			date > 2009.2.1
			date > 2013.2.1
			date > 2017.2.1
			date > 2021.2.1
		}

	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	timeout_days = 1
	immediate = {
		if = { #8th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2001.1.1
					date < 2002.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.2
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #9th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2005.1.1
					date < 2006.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.3
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #10th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2009.1.1
					date < 2010.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #11th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2013.1.1
					date < 2014.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #12th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2017.1.1
					date < 2018.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.6
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #13th Period
			limit = {
					date > 2021.1.1
					date < 2022.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.7
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.1.a executed"
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category
	}
}

	trigger = {
		has_government = communism
		OR = {
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
		tag = PER
		date > 2005.3.1
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	timeout_days = 30
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ahmadinejad
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_raisi
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_tavakoli
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ghalibaf
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_rezaee
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_hemmati
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_khatami
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_mousavi
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rafsanjani
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rouhani

		set_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		set_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ahmadinejad
		set_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rafsanjani
		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = PER_auto_update_gui_weekly
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.3.a executed"
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category
	}

		}

	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	timeout_days = 30
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ahmadinejad
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_raisi
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_tavakoli
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ghalibaf
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_rezaee
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_hemmati
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_khatami
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_mousavi
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rafsanjani
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rouhani

		set_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
		set_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ghalibaf
		set_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rouhani
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = PER_auto_update_gui_weekly
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = PER_election_events.21
					days = 20
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					30 = { # 30% Chance that Ghalibaf withdraws with historical AI off
					country_event = {
						id = PER_election_events.21
						days = 20
					}
					}
					70 = { }
				}
			}
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.5.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.5.a executed"
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category
	}
}

country_event = { # Khatami Elected as President 2001 (Reformists Won)
	id = PER_election_events.8
	title = PER_election_events.8.t
	desc = PER_election_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_khatami_won_election
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.8.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.8.a executed"

		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes

		set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 8 }
		change_ruling_party_effect = yes

		PER_scripted_effect_finish_election = yes
		set_country_flag = PER_president_khatami # Set President
		add_to_variable = { iranian_president_change = 1 }
		add_ideas = PER_khatami_idea
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {

				}
				country_event = {
					id = PER_election_events.28
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	title = PER_election_events.22.t
	desc = PER_election_events.22.d
	picture = GFX_politics_talks
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = { #Let's do this!
		name = PER_election_events.22.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.22.a executed"
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 9 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
			30 = {
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 8 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
		}
		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
	}
	option = { #Nevermind.
		name = PER_election_events.22.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.22.b executed"
		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
	}
}

	desc = PER_election_events.28.desc
	picture = GFX_election_protests
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Suppress them now!
		name = PER_election_events.28.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.28.a executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_harsh_protests_tt
		add_ideas = PER_harsh_protests
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = PER_harsh_protests
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = PER_harsh_protests
				days = 25
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Let Principalists storm!
		name = PER_election_events.28.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.28.b executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_protests_tt
		add_ideas = PER_protests
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = PER_protests
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = PER_protests
				days = 90
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # This will pass like the others...
		name = PER_election_events.28.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.28.c executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_peaceful_protests_tt
		add_ideas = PER_peaceful_protests
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = PER_peaceful_protests
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = PER_peaceful_protests
				days = 130
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Ok sure, there was fraud in the election.
		name = PER_election_events.28.d
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.28.d executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_mousavi_becomes_president_tt
		set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 8 }
		change_ruling_party_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			PER_scripted_effect_finish_election = yes
			set_country_flag = PER_president_mousavi # Set President
			add_to_variable = { iranian_president_change = 1 }
			add_ideas = PER_mousavi_idea
		}
	}
}

				planning_skill = 2
				logistics_skill = 3

				traits = { trait_engineer }
				skill = 4
				attack_skill = 4
				defense_skill = 3
				planning_skill = 3
				logistics_skill = 3
			}
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Ali Hajilo"
				portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/PER/Army_Gen_Ali_Hajilo.dds"
				traits = { desert_fox }
				skill = 4

			}

			news_event = {
				id = PER_rev_flavor.1
				days = 40
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 18 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.25 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.25 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				clear_array = ruling_party
				clear_array = gov_coalition_array
				add_to_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
				update_government_coalition_strength = yes
				set_coalition_drift = yes
				set_ruling_leader = yes
				set_leader = yes
				set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				start_civil_war = {
					clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
					set_cosmetic_tag = PER_mullahs_government
					ideology = communism
					keep_political_leader = yes
					keep_political_party_members = yes
					size = 0.35
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = PER
					NOT = { has_state_flag = PER_locals_swayed }
				}
				set_state_flag = PER_locals_not_swayed
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = PER_mullahs_government
				ideology = communism
				size = army_size_jang
				capital = 402
				states = all
				states_filter = {
					has_state_flag = PER_locals_not_swayed
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Referendum
	id = PER_revolution.301
	title = PER_revolution.301.t
	desc = PER_revolution.301.d
	picture = GFX_political_deal

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Democracy
		name = PER_revolution.301.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_sway.301.a executed"
		news_event = {
			id = PER_rev_flavor.9
			days = 1
		}
		complete_national_focus = PER_democracy
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.35 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.35 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_array = ruling_party
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
			add_to_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
			update_government_coalition_strength = yes
			set_coalition_drift = yes
			set_ruling_leader = yes
			set_leader = yes
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_global_flag = PER_PAN_PERSIA
			}
		}
	}
